e
nsa has been imposed on the accused who attacked BJP MLA Yogesh Verma on the day of Holi in Lakhimpur Kheri district of Uttar Pradesh
 court ne mukhya aaropee sahit teen khanan mafiaon par enese lagaaya he
 Let me tell you that on the day of Holi, BJP MLA from Lakhimpur Sadar seat Yogesh Verma was standing by his side along the road, when a person involved in mining business came to him after getting down from the car and after some saying he sat back in his car
 
 iske fouran baad usne bijepi vidhayak ke pair main goli maar di thi
 CCTV footage of the BJP MLA shot was revealed, based on which the police took action and demanded imposition of NSA on 3 people including the main accused
 ab enese lagane ke baad yah teenon khanan mafia 1 saal tak jail main hi bithaayenge
 Of the three accused in the mining business accused of shooting Yogesh Verma, 2 are currently lodged in Lakhimpur Jail and 1 Bahraich jail has been transferred

 ramanaidu ko aktubar main goa main bhartiya antarrashtriya filmotsav ke dauraan yah puraskaar bhent kiya jayega
 As a prize, he will be presented a Swarna Kamal, a cash prize of ten lakh rupees and a shawl
 unhen yah puraskaar bhartiya cinema main unke ullekhneey yogadan ke liye diya ja rahaa he
 Born in 1936 in Karamchedu in Prakasam district in Andhra Pradesh, Ramanaidu entered the film world in 1963 with his debut film Anuragam
 iske baad 1964 main unki duusari film ramudu-bheemudu ai
 The film starring NT Rama Rao was a superhit
 unka filmi safar 47 saal main failaa he

 unhone hindi, bengali, oriya, asamiya, malayalam, tamil, kannada, gujarati, marathi or bhojpuri sahit kai bhashaaon main filmein banaai

 " is november tak 33 karod pan dharakon main se 13

devi kaa yah swaroop param shantidaayak or kalyankari he
